 - That's why the Perfect Relations of the Consultant Agency already working with the Delhi Government were asked whether they were able to do this work? - Perfect Relations said that Google, Facebook, youtube are the medium, There is no competition
 ye duniya bhar main apni tarah kii iklauti companiyaan he

 - kansaltent company parfect relation ne kaha ki google, fasebuk, utyub se unke dwaara nirdhaarit rate par ye kaam wo kara sakati he
 - Consultant Company Perfect Relations gave its proposal on 6 July
 - sarkaar ne parfect relation ko ye kaam nimna 3 sharton ke saath diya
 - Consultant company will give an intertexting that the rates fixed by Facebook, youtube and Google are minimum and non-negotiable
 kansaltent company in companiyon se kisi bhi tarah kii riyasat, chhot yaa kamishan nahin legi or agar kansaltent ko kisi tarah kii riyasat, chhot yaa kamishan yaa or kisi bhi tarah kaa phayda miltaa he, to vah uske bilon se kaat liya jayega
 - For this work, the consultant company will not be given any kind of charge except the terms and conditions available with the contract with DIP

 yah isliye karnaa padaa kyonki 1954 main 8 jajon kii bench ne or 1962 main 6 jajon kii bench yah faisla suna chuki he ki niztaa kaa adhikaar nahin hota

 ye peeth do dinon tak sunwaayee karegi
